This is a great feature for ESL students in IELTS preparation. \r\n\r\n\r\nHow can I save word status for future use? \r\nIELTS Words in 30 Days will save word status at your computer or device for future use automatically. Whenever you select a right answer in word quiz, the word's status will be set as Passed, otherwise it will be as New. \r\n\r\n\r\nIs there any difference among this Windows 8 Store version and other versions? \r\nAll versions of IELTS Words in 30 Days from Pacific Lava English School share same word list in general. We commonly update word list and its definitions per year, but cannot update all versions at same day, so at particular period there is tiny difference possibly among these versions. As for software features, separate versions have different merits based on the natures of various devices, users can select on demand. \r\n\r\n\r\nWhy do I have to be online when doing word quiz or showing word list of the day? \r\nIELTS Words in 30 Days keep your own studying data at local device. However, it produces word quiz, word explanation, and word list of the day dynamically through Internet. Any network failure would stop the app. It is why you have to keep online when running the app. \r\n\r\n\r\nSometimes I find out that the word quiz is different from previous one, why? \r\nIn most cases, the app will keep word quiz in memory. But there are 2 exceptions. If you close the app and restart it, the quiz will be refreshed and would be different from previous one.
